     "- **Overall arrangement**: [Description of how fruits are arranged on the tablecloth]"\n    )\n    \n    # Prepare API request\n    api_key = os.getenv(\'OPENAI_API_KEY\')\n    api_base = \n                    print(\'\\n\' + \'=\'*80)\n                    print(\'=== GPT-4O VISUAL ANALYSIS RESULTS ===\')\n                    print(\'=\'*80)\n
